class="overlayTrigger"><button class="btn btn-link v-medium author-button" type="button" data-track="Nickname Stats" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="2ccdb60c-d8f1-3105-ad3a-b0a2c62a2c47"><div class="ugc-author v-fw-medium body-copy-lg"><strong>Bryan</strong></div></button></span></span><div class="visible-xs visible-sm in-header"><div class="feature-ratings"><h4 class="features-heading">Features</h4><div class="rating-bars"><div class="quality-rating rating-group"><div class="rating-description">Quality</div><div class="bars-group"><div class="sr-only">5 out of 5</div><div class="rating-bar filled first "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled last "></div></div></div><div class="value-rating rating-group"><div class="rating-description">Value</div><div class="bars-group"><div class="sr-only">5 out of 5</div><div class="rating-bar filled first "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled last "></div></div></div><div class="ease-of-use-rating rating-group"><div class="rating-description">Ease of Use</div><div class="bars-group"><div class="sr-only">5 out of 5</div><div class="rating-bar filled first "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled last "></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ugc-review-body body-copy-lg"><p class="pre-white-space">Great GPU for 4K gaming. There is a little bit of coil whine on mine in very high fps situations (300+) but it's not noticeable in most cases. HDMI 2.1 has allowed my LG B9 OLED to use GSYNC and 4K @ 120hz. This has been great. Most games that I've played I've been able to get 120fps after tuning the settings a bit. 

The two slot design is probably the best feature of this vs the other styles of 3080 in my opinion. I wouldn't have been able to fit the others in my case which can only support a 2 slot graphics card. 

Buying one was extremely difficult. I spent almost 2 months trying to buy one. Great GPU I just wish nvidia would have had some supply at launch, hopefully this improves soon.</p></div><div class="in-review"><div class="feature-ratings"><h4 viewBox="0 0 87 16" fill="#C5CBD5" preserveAspectRatio="xMinYMin slice"><use href="/~assets/bby/_img/int/plsvgdef-frontend/svg/star-rating-empty.svg#star-rating-empty" xlink:href="/~assets/bby/_img/int/plsvgdef-frontend/svg/star-rating.svg#star-rating"></use></svg></span></i></div></div><h4 class="review-title c-section-title heading-5 v-fw-medium  " id="review-id-d9797f84-9450-3ecb-8356-f9019388f9f9">Big improvement over the 1080ti</h4></div><div class="review-context"><div class="verified-purchaser-mv-wrapper"><span class="c-overlay-wrapper"><span class="overlayTrigger"><button class="btn btn-link v-medium ugc-components verified-purchaser-badge" type="button" data-track="Verified Purchase Badge" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="verified-purchase-badge-overlay"><img alt="" aria-hidden="true" src="https://www.bestbuy.com/~assets/bby/_com/ugc-raas/ugc-common-assets/ugc-badge-verified-check.svg"/>Verified Purchase</button></span></span><span class="context-divider">|</span></div><div class="disclaimer">Posted <time class="submission-date" title="Dec 8, 2020 12:43 PM">2 weeks ago</time>.</div><div class="length-of-ownership">Owned for <!-- -->3 weeks<!-- --> when reviewed.</div></div><div class="lv-heading"><div class="visible-xs visible-sm"><span class="c-overlay-wrapper"><span class="overlayTrigger"><button class="btn btn-link v-medium author-button" type="button" data-track="Nickname Stats" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="d9797f84-9450-3ecb-8356-f9019388f9f9"><div class="ugc-author v-fw-medium body-copy-lg"><strong>cafish</strong></div></button></span></span><div class="visible-xs visible-sm in-header"><div class="feature-ratings"><h4 class="features-heading">Features</h4><div class="rating-bars"><div class="quality-rating rating-group"><div class="rating-description">Quality</div><div class="bars-group"><div class="sr-only">5 out of 5</div><div class="rating-bar filled first "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled last "></div></div></div><div class="value-rating rating-group"><div class="rating-description">Value</div><div class="bars-group"><div class="sr-only">4 out of 5</div><div class="rating-bar filled first "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar  last "></div></div></div><div class="ease-of-use-rating rating-group"><div class="rating-description">Ease of Use</div><div class="bars-group"><div class="sr-only">5 out of 5</div><div class="rating-bar filled first "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled  "></div><div class="rating-bar filled last "></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ugc-review-body body-copy-lg"><p class="pre-white-space">Upgrading from sli 2x 1080ti I didn't think I would see a huge improvement. I was wrong. 
 This card is much better at handling high rez and high fps, all while staying in the 70s, something my 1080ti's did not do well. Dlss 2.0 is great if you can keep it in the "quality" setting, it gives a significant fps boost and adds smoothness to your games. Personally, the Dlss is my favorite feature of this card, and I hope more games use it in the future. Ray-tracing looks very good on this card, but I'm still hesitant to use it fully on games that higher fps is preferred. The card is very quiet for me and it's idle temp is usually 26c. By default settings, the fans on this card do not even spin until it warms up to over 30c. Under load and stress tests, I was able to hit a max of 76c. Under the same tests' I have hit over 90c+ and thermal throttled on my 1080ti's. Also wanted to mention that my particular 3080 has zero coil whine, so overall, very quiet and cool. 

If I have one negative thing to say about this gpu, It's the power cable. The card has a great look with it's minimal rgb (which is controllable in iQUE) but the power cable plugs into it at an awkward spot close to the middle and covers up the white geforce logo. I bought the evga adapter plug and it looks much better with it, but the adapter that this card comes with is not the best looking. 

Overall, I'm very satisfied with this gpu. I highly recommend it if you can get it at msrp. Nvidia or AMD would have to make a very significant leap before I consider upgrading this.</p></div><div class="in-review"><div class="feature-ratings"><h4 class="features-heading">Features</h4><div body-copy-lg"><p class="pre-white-space">After missing out on this card for so many times because it went out of stock right before I pressed the Place Order button, I was finally able to get one and trust me, it felt like a big achievement beating all the bots to get one. When the card got delivered,  it came with deinflated air cushions (I have heard almost everyone is getting this card from Best Buy the same way). Luckily the card was intact and damage free, thanks to very good cushioning inside the box by NVidia.

With those struggles out of the way I would like to talk about the actual functioning of the card. I game at 1440p and it might seem like an overkill for that. But I am able to get close to 60fps give or take with GeForce Experience optimized settings for Watch Dogs Legion (My CPU is i9 9900k OC 5GHz all cores)

I also played Control with DLSS 2.0 On (Which is another great thing about NVidia cards) and I was easily able to hit 100FPS+ with great visuals (I could not visually see any difference between DLSS upscaled and native 1440p resolutions).

Crysis Remastered at high settings was also hitting close to 90FPS.

I upgraded from EVGA xc3 ultra 2080S to this and I must say, it was a great great upgrade for me. The card runs at around 80 C while playing Watch Dogs Legion which is more than my 2080S but I guess is okay because it stays in the upper frequency bins for almost all the time.

As for the card design, the build quality is top notch and the card feels heavy because of its beefy cooling solution (dont take it in a negative sense, the card is compact with its 2 slot design for the power it can produce). Only thing that bothers me is the power cable adapter from NVidia that just makes the whole setup look ugly.</p></div><div class="in-review"><div class="feature-ratings"><h4 id="Question-3430a7ef-8b9a-31e5-b9fd-8befd809141a">I currently have the NVIDIA GeForce 1060 GTX 3GB. Will I be able to replace it with this beauty? 
I hope itll fit in my iBUYPOWER PC.</a></h4><p class="author"><span class="asked-ago">Asked <time class="submission-date" title="Sep 6, 2020 1:13 PM">3 months ago</time> by<!-- --> <!-- -->Gingy94<!-- -->.</span></p><div class="image-carousel"><div class="nav-wrapper false false page-size-eight"><ul class="image-list no-nav"><li><a class="selected" data-track="QnA: Question: Image" href="javascript:void(0)" role="button"><img alt="Thats my PC., click to load a larger version" src="https://photos-us.bazaarvoice.com/photo/2/cGhvdG86YmVzdGJ1eQ/a56faacb-9291-5f21-985f-f8d6e080ddbc"/></a></li></ul></div></div><ul class="answers"><li class="answer"><div class="answer-text" data-answer-id="5c8dd043-b796-3359-868c-85ea926ec66d" id="answer-id-5c8dd043-b796-3359-868c-85ea926ec66d" tabindex="-1"><div class="ugc-components line-clamp"><div class="undefined fade-out "><span aria-hidden="true" class="v-fw-medium">A:</span><span class="sr-only">Answer</span><span>You'll have to bust out a tape measure, the RTX 3080 measure in at 11.2"(L) x 4.4" (W), which is much larger length wise than the 1060 which is only 6.8" (L). Side note, the RTX 3080 is a 350 watt card, the 1060 is only 230 watts, you'll also need to confirm your power supply can handle that. 700 watt or more is recommended and it needs 2x 8 pin pci-e plugs (with included adapter) or a new power supply with the very recently adopted 12 pin pci-e plug</span></div><button class="btn btn-link v-medium btn-read-more read-more-button" type="button" role="presentation"/></div></li><li class="question-list-item"><div class="question-answer"><h4 class="question-title"><span aria-hidden="true" class="v-fw-medium">Q:</span><span class="sr-only">Question</span><a data-track="QnA: Single Question Page" href="/site/questions/nvidia-geforce-rtx-3080-10gb-gddr6x-pci-express-4-0-graphics-card-titanium-and-black/6429440/question/69df04b1-4ca8-3656-88d4-d11193e0e505" id="Question-69df04b1-4ca8-3656-88d4-d11193e0e505">Will this card ever come back out if so when</a></h4><p class="author"><span class="asked-ago">Asked <time class="submission-date" title="Dec 5, 2020 10:57 PM">3 weeks ago</time> by<!-- --> <!-- -->Bob<!-- -->.</span></p><ul class="answers"><li class="answer"><div class="answer-text" data-answer-id="7c52266a-b37e-363a-a724-1a3297e6d545" id="answer-id-7c52266a-b37e-363a-a724-1a3297e6d545" tabindex="-1"><div class="ugc-components line-clamp"><div class="undefined fade-out "><span aria-hidden="true" class="v-fw-medium">A:</span><span class="sr-only">Answer</span><span>They *will* come back out, but expect no forewarning announcement whatsoever. There is no definitive answer from BestBuy on this, and their reason is understandable, but frustrating. Restocks are the best-kept secret of this card. Giving no lead warning is policy for BestBuy, as a mechanism for detecting and subsequently at-least-trying-before-failing to eliminate bots. If the scalpers running bot armies know no more than you do, they are forced to perpetually hammer the site to detect stock change 24/7, and in so doing become more "visible" for BestBuys anti-botting detection and supposed blacklisting. Honestly, however, it doesn't do much good at all. This site, and specifically this page, are assaulted non-stop by bots disguising and/or masquerading IP info, etc. When they do come back in stock the bots cart them all within seconds, even with BestBuys "Second phase" authentication. 


That said, for what it is worth, I've watched in earnest since launch, and have worn out the label of my F5 key. BestBuy *appears* to restock every 1.5 to 2.5 weeks. The latest restock came in 1-week + 5-days after the prior. There is no specific day (Friday seems to be the most common, but I've seen Wednesday twice, and even a Monday), nor specific time (I've seen 6:00AM PST, 8:00AM PST, and 2:00PM PST). At the time of this answer being authored the last restock was 2020-12-02, a Wednesday, at 8:00am PST, and they were literally gone in seconds (less than ten). I managed to get to "second phase" authentication before the page hung indefinitely and eventually timed out, several times. It took another 25 minutes before the site finally hung out the DND sign, and proceeded to flip back and forth between "Coming Soon" and "Sold Out" a half dozen times during the subsequent two hours before finally settling on what you see now (Sold Out). The prior restock happened on 2020-11-20, a Friday, at 6:00am PST, and was also wiped out in seconds, with a similar experience on my part.


There is no notify system; there is no wait-list. If you want it you have to be on the site, and have loaded the page to see the restock within seconds of it going live, or you're going to miss it (and, as I described earlier, even then, you'll likely still miss it). It is battle-royale, every man/woman/child/bot for themselves (one of those clearly having a distinct advantage).</span></div><button class="btn btn-link v-medium btn-read-more read-more-button" type="button" data-track="QnA: Answer: Read More" aria-describedby="7c52266a-b37e-363a-a724-1a3297e6d545">Read more <svg aria-hidden="true" role="img" viewBox="0 0 100 100"><use href="/~assets/bby/_img/int/plsvgdef-frontend/svg/Caret_Down_Line_Sm.svg#Caret_Down_Line_Sm" xlink:href="/~assets/bby/_img/int/plsvgdef-frontend/svg/Caret_Down_Line_Sm.svg#Caret_Down_Line_Sm"></use></svg></button></div></div><p class="author">Answered <time class="submission-date" title="Dec
